                            </p>
                            <h3>Wireless Sync</h3>
                            <p>
                                The device syncs wirelessly anytime you're relatively motionless within 15 feet of an active base station.

                            <p>

<script>
(function() {
    if(window.fitbit){
        fitbit.namespace("fitbit.app.googleAnalytics");
    }else{
        window.fitbit={app:{}}
    }


    fitbit.app.googleAnalytics = {
        deferredCookieName : "gaDeferred",
        eventParamDelimiter : ",",

        getEnvironment: function(host) {
            if (host.indexOf("local") == 0) {
                return "dev";
            } else if (host.indexOf("qa3") == 0) {
                return "qa3";
            } else if (host.indexOf("qa2") == 0) {
                return "qa2";
            } else if (host.indexOf("qa1") == 0) {
                return "qa1";
            } else {
                return "prod"
            }
        },

        deferredTracking: function() {
            var deferredCookieName = fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.deferredCookieName;
            var eventsData = fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.parseGAData(deferredCookieName);
            if(eventsData != null) {
                for (trackEventName in eventsData) {
                    try {
                        var trackEventString = eventsData[trackEventName];
                        var trackEventData = trackEventString.split( fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.eventParamDelimiter );
                        //log event
                        _gaq.push([ "_trackEvent" , trackEventData[0] , trackEventData[1] , trackEventData[2] ]);
                    } catch(e) {

                    }
                }
                var expires = new Date();
                document.cookie = fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.deferredCookieName + "=" + "; expires=" +
                        expires.toGMTString() + "; path=/";
            }
        },

        parseGAData: function( cookieName ) {
            var cookiesString = document.cookie;
            if (cookiesString) {
                var searchPart = fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.deferredCookieName + "=";
                var gaCookieStartIndex = cookiesString.indexOf(searchPart);
                var table = null;
                while (gaCookieStartIndex != -1) {
                    var gaCookieEndIndex = cookiesString.indexOf(";",gaCookieStartIndex);
                    var gaCookieString = null;
                    if (gaCookieEndIndex != -1) {
                        gaCookieString = cookiesString.substring(gaCookieStartIndex,gaCookieEndIndex);
                    } else {
                        gaCookieString = cookiesString.substring(gaCookieStartIndex);
                        gaCookieEndIndex = gaCookieStartIndex + gaCookieString.length;
                    }
                    if (gaCookieStartIndex + searchPart.length < gaCookieEndIndex) {
                        //get actual query string
                        var query = gaCookieString.substring(searchPart.length);
                        var parsed = fitbit.app.googleAnalytics.parseCookiePart(query);
                        if (table == null) {
                            table = parsed;
                        } else if(parsed != null) {
                            for (property in parsed) {
                                table[property] = parsed[property];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    gaCookieStartIndex = cookiesString.indexOf(searchPart,gaCookieEndIndex);
                }
                //remove cookie
                return table;
            }
            return null;
        },

        parseCookiePart: function( query ) {
            var queryParts = decodeURIComponent(query).split("&");
            var queryPart  = null;
            if (queryParts.length > 0) {
                var table = new Object();
                for (var i = 0 , len = queryParts.length; i < len; i++) {
                    queryPart = queryParts[i].split("=");
                    table[decodeURIComponent(queryPart[0])] = decodeURIComponent(queryPart[1]);
                }
                return table;
            }
            return null;
        }
    };

    /* acct is GA account number, i.e. "UA-5555555-1" */
    function gaSSDSLoad(acct) {
        if (!window._gaq) {
            window._gaq = [];
        }
        var _gaq = window._gaq;
        _gaq.push(['_setAccount', acct]);
        if(document.domain) {
            _gaq.push(['_setDomainName', document.domain]);
        }
        _gaq.push(['_setAllowLinker', true]);

        _gaq.push(['_setCustomVar', 1, "visitorType", "trackerUser", 1]);
        _gaq.push(['_setCustomVar', 2, "country", "en_US", 1]);

        var pageURI = window.location.pathname;

            //async loading of GA code
            var gaJsHost = (("https:" == document.location.protocol) ? "https://ssl." : "http://www.");
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = gaJsHost + 'google-analytics.com/ga.js';
            script.type = 'text/javascript';
            script.async = true;
            script.onloadDone = false;
            script.onload = function () {
                script.onloadDone = true;

        }
